Xiaoshan Unfilial Son Assaults Elderly Mother 84

Zhang Xiaomao, from the Xiangyi Fang in the western countryside of Xiaoshan, was originally a farmer, but he was addicted to gambling. After his father passed away in the spring, Zhang became even more reckless, selling off the family's fields and squandering the proceeds. He often clashed with his mother, demanding money. On the 30th of last month, he demanded money from his mother again, and when she refused, he severely beat his elderly mother, who was over seventy years old. His mother, in despair, attempted suicide by drowning herself in the river. Fortunately, a fishing boat spotted her and managed to rescue her, but she was barely breathing. The villagers are indignant and have filed a lawsuit with the county, requesting that he be severely punished.

Large Number of Refugees Disturbing Four Townships 85

On the afternoon of the 30th, more than a hundred refugees from Jiangxi arrived in Xinfawang, in the eastern countryside of Xiaoshan. They were supporting the old and carrying the young, looking very miserable. They first went to each household, forcibly demanding money and rice. If their demands were not met, they would smash things indiscriminately, terrifying the people. Fortunately, the township police gathered some money and rice, and they dispersed. Unexpectedly, dozens more refugees arrived the next day, engaging in robbery. Fortunately, the water police suppressed them and expelled them from the area, and nothing further happened.

Qingjiang Business Community Issues Circulation Coupons 86

Merchants in various industries in Huaiyin have recently felt the shortage of copper coins, hindering turnover in retail trade, which has greatly affected business. They specially selected representatives from each industry to find relief measures. After discussion, it was proposed to temporarily issue 50,000 qián of circulation coupons, which were not used in the relief of the money shortage in December of the 19th year of the Republic, to facilitate turnover. Each industry would raise 17,000 yuan in cash as a reserve fund. A management and guarantee committee would be organized, with managers of reputable stores in each industry serving as committee members. A preparatory meeting will be held again today (the 30th) at 2:00 PM to submit the plan to the party and government agencies for filing.

Shanghai Car Causes Trouble in Hangzhou 88

Local News

Shanghai-Fujian Telegraph Line Restored Yesterday; Rumors of Contact in Northern Fujian Untrue 89

According to the Xinxin News Agency, the sudden interruption of the Shanghai-Fujian telegraph line the night before last led to rumors of contact between Liu Heding's troops and the 19th Route Army in northern Fujian, causing alarm and tension. A reporter from the Xinxin News Agency inquired at the Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications yesterday morning and learned that the Shanghai-Fujian telegraph line had been interrupted briefly due to the telegraph line touching the telephone line around 8:00 PM last night (the night before last). It has now been repaired and is functioning as usual. Therefore, the rumor of contact in northern Fujian was a misunderstanding.

Tang Youren Discusses Central Government's Use of Force Against Fujian; Sealing Fujian Ports Met with Protests from Various Countries; We Have Requested All Japanese Residents to Evacuate 90

It is rumored that Tang Youren, the Secretary-General of the Central Political Committee, came to Shanghai to discuss methods for handling the Fujian situation with central committee members in Shanghai. The central government has no other suitable method other than using force against Fujian. Sealing the ports has not been effectively implemented, and various countries have opposed it. The following is a record of Tang's remarks:

Purely Personal Matters 91

Tang stated that his visit was purely for personal matters and that he did not have the task of discussing solutions to the Fujian situation with central committee members in Shanghai. He had family matters that urgently needed to be addressed, so he took a flight to Shanghai yesterday, causing special attention from the outside world. On the central government's side, it is believed that the Fujian issue cannot be resolved politically. Chen and others have betrayed the country and overthrown the party's rule. The central government can only adopt military methods to quickly quell the rebellion and prevent the spread of red terror. It is now reported that there is severe internal strife and division within the Fujian faction, which may avoid the outbreak of war.

Difficult to Invade Zhejiang 92

It is untrue that clashes have already occurred in northern Fujian. It is difficult for the Fujian army to transport troops because the mountain roads in northern Fujian are rugged, the water flow is rapid, and transportation is inconvenient. Reports that the Fujian faction will still follow Sun Chuanfang's old route into Zhejiang are also not easy. Previously, when Sun advanced from Fuzhou, it took six days of walking to reach the border of Zhejiang. It is too early to say that clashes have occurred in northern Fujian. There is no such speed. As for the central army advancing towards Fujian, it will be easy to march because they are in a commanding position.

Sealing Negotiations 93

The maritime blockade of Fujian has been in effect for a few days, with inspections of incoming and outgoing ships. Various countries are currently engaging in negotiations with us on this matter. Japan is using the pretext of protecting Japanese residents. We have requested all Japanese residents to evacuate. However, Japan believes that the losses from evacuating so many people would be too great and has not been able to implement it. Currently, there are 20,000 Taiwanese and over a thousand Japanese in Fujian. As for foreigners, there are four French citizens who are working as professors and are quite safe, which is not a problem.

Yang Dezao Discusses Visit to Jiangxi to Meet Chiang; Reports on Situation in the South Without Negotiations; Fujian Uprising Affects Communist Suppression in Jiangxi 94

According to the Far East News Agency, Yang Dezao, the representative of Chen Jitang, the Commander-in-Chief of the Communist Suppression in the South, returned from northern Guangdong a month ago and, under Chen's orders, passed through Nanjing to visit Chiang in Jiangxi. He took a China National Aviation Corporation plane back to Nanjing the day before yesterday and then took the 5:25 PM express train to Shanghai that afternoon. A reporter from the Far East News Agency interviewed him at his residence on Avenue Amre yesterday and recorded the following:

Chiang-Chen Meeting Completely Untrue 95

Yang, in response to the reporter's question, first stated that his visit to Jiangxi to meet Chairman Chiang was to report on the military situation of the Communist Suppression in the South and that there was no so-called negotiation. Reports that Chairman Chiang and Chen Bonan (Jitang) met in Nanfeng previously are completely untrue. However, it is true that Chen and He Jian, the Chairman of Hunan, met in Lechang, but it was only to discuss military strategies for suppressing the communists.

No News of Hu Forming a Government 96

He continued to say that he had only seen reports about Hu Hanmin forming another government in the southwest and had not heard anything about it. He had not heard any such rumors when he passed through Hong Kong from Guangdong last time. As for the joint telegram sent by the Southwest Executive Department and the Southwest Political Committee to the central government with some kind of expression, he had not seen the telegram and did not know its implications. However, based on what he knew in the past, Chen Bonan and others have always sympathized with the central government. Their response to the Fujian uprising should be in line with the central government's actions.

Communist Suppression Affected by Fujian 97

He also stated that eight months ago, when he was in Nanchang, he still had some doubts about the central government's plan for suppressing the communists. After staying in Nanchang for a week and talking to officers of all levels, he deeply understood that the military operation to suppress the communists was very promising. Although it was not possible to completely wipe them out within two months as Chairman Chiang had said, it was certainly not difficult to completely wipe them out within at least four to six months. The communist forces have two major shortcomings: a lack of supplies and difficulty in replenishment. Especially since the implementation of the blockade policy, the communist areas have felt an increasing panic about supplies. In addition, the communist suppression forces have won successive victories in recent months, and the communist forces have been unable to replenish their ranks due to heavy casualties. If the communist suppression forces are not restrained, their eradication can be expected soon. However, the uprising in Fujian has opened a door for the communists, providing them with supplies and resources. As a result, the military operation to suppress the communists has been greatly affected, which is truly heartbreaking. Yang finally stated that he had no mission on this visit to Shanghai, would stay for a day or two, and then return to Nanjing.

Former Chief of Staff of the Garrison Headquarters Zhang Xiang Returns to Shanghai for Discussions; Visit to Chen and Chiang Unsuccessful, Advice Ignored; Two Meetings with Dai Ji Held at Banquets; Commercial Market in Fuzhou Further Depressed by the Uprising 98

According to the Guowen News Agency, Zhang Xiang, the former Chief of Staff of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, followed Dai Ji for many years. After Dai resigned as commander and traveled to North China, he went to Fujian. Shortly after, Zhang also resigned from his position in Shanghai and went to Fujian to sweep the tombs. Zhang suddenly returned the other day, leading to rumors that Dai and Zhang disagreed with the policies of the Fujian province, and that Dai had been detained by Fujian. Yesterday, a reporter visited Zhang's residence on Jin Shenfu Road, where Zhang granted an interview. The following is a record of the conversation:

Visiting Tombs in Fujian 99

When Zhang met the reporter, he first stated that after resigning from his position at the Garrison Headquarters, he was invited by friends from other places. However, he had not returned to Minhou, his hometown, since leaving in 1927. So, he decided to take advantage of the tomb-sweeping opportunity and return to Fujian. He departed from Shanghai on the 15th of last month and arrived in Fuzhou on the 17th. At that time, he had only heard rumors of the Fujian uprising, not seen any actual events. He originally planned to return to Shanghai after finishing the tomb-sweeping and taking care of family matters, and then respond to the invitation of a friend. However, after completing the tomb-sweeping, Fujian actually declared independence. Seeing this situation, he knew it would be difficult to stay any longer and took the Jisheng ship, which departed from Fuzhou directly, in the late last month and came directly to Shanghai. Chen Tianjing, the commander of the naval training camp who escaped, also came to Shanghai on the same ship. Therefore, Zhang had already been in Shanghai for several days.

Meeting Chen and Chiang 100

Zhang also said that when he arrived in Fuzhou on the 17th, he heard that there would be changes in Fujian Province. Chen Mingshu and Jiang Guangnai were his former superiors, so he went to visit Chen and Chiang. At that time, he immediately saw that internal and external troubles were coming one after another. If the domestic political situation changed again, the country would be torn apart. He presented his opinions to Chen and Chiang. However, at that time, the Fujian faction had already made up its mind, and he was a person of little importance. How could he make anyone change their mind? Seeing that the matter was difficult to reverse, he went to the countryside the next day to sweep the tombs and take care of personal matters. After the matter was completed, he saw that the situation had changed greatly and returned quickly. He did not stay in Fujian for a long time.

Recent Situation in Fuzhou 101

The situation in Fuzhou, such as commerce, has been deteriorating in recent years. Minhou is the location of the provincial capital, and public security is still considered peaceful. However, under the conditions of rural bankruptcy and economic depression in China, the market was already depressed. Now, after this change, the economy has become even more depressed. A sense of terror has not yet appeared.

Two Meetings with Dai 102

Finally, the reporter asked about the rumors that Dai had been detained by the Fujian faction. According to Zhang, he met Commander Dai twice in Fujian, but the meetings were all at private banquets. Every time he wanted to ask Dai something, Dai would raise his glass and say, "Please, please." So he did not ask. After the banquet, Dai stayed at Chairman Jiang's (Guangnai) residence, and the gate of Jiang's residence was heavily guarded, so it was inconvenient to disturb him. Now he has returned to Shanghai for several days, so he does not dare to speculate on the details. When asked if he would soon leave Shanghai to go to Nanjing or to answer the call of a friend, he replied that he was temporarily taking care of family affairs in Shanghai and would not leave Shanghai or go to Nanjing. After the conversation, they parted ways.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Submits Request to City Government to Intervene in the Arrest of Kim Seok; Kim Seok's Father Issues Statement; Naturalized as Chinese Citizen in 1929 109

After Kim Seok, a Korean who had naturalized as a Chinese citizen, was arrested in the French Concession on November 22, more than 360 citizens, including Zhang Yiqing and Li Yannian, sent letters to various organizations requesting assistance. The public has paid close attention to this issue. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce immediately submitted a request to the municipal government for serious intervention to protect him. At the same time, Kim Seok's father, Kim Young-dak (name: Cheol), issued an emergency statement to the Xinsheng News Agency, stating the process of naturalization with the permission of the Chinese government. The details are as follows:

Petition from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce 110

This petition concerns a request. It has been observed that the Japanese have been enticing and arresting Korean nationals who have naturalized as Chinese citizens almost constantly over the past year. However, there has been no satisfactory resolution or strict negotiation. Which Korean national would be willing to naturalize as Chinese again, only to court uncertainty? When Japanese consuls arrest people in Chinese territory, they should request our officials to transfer the arrested according to treaty extradition measures. If arrests occur in the concession, considering that the Korean national has already naturalized as Chinese, the case should be handled by the Second Special District Court according to the court agreement method, not unilaterally by the Japanese consulate. Furthermore, if they proceed with enticement and arrest without first consulting the French Concession, it constitutes an infringement of the French Concession's police authority, and the French consul should not condone it. The case of Jin Yongduo last year serves as a precedent. It is appropriate to prepare a document and submit it to your esteemed government for review, and to request a thorough investigation and strict negotiation. This would be a matter of public benefit.

Jin Yongduo's Statement 111

Jin Yongduo (Che) makes an urgent statement to the reporter of the News Society regarding the illegal arrest of his eldest son, Xi. The statement begins: Although Che was born in Korea, he was permitted to naturalize by the Chinese government on October 5th of the 18th year of the Republic of China, holding Permit No. 67, which serves as proof. Therefore, since October of the 18th year of the Republic of China, the entire Che family has obtained Chinese nationality. In other words, they are purely Chinese citizens. As Chinese citizens, they should be protected by Chinese law. There is no doubt that, according to international norms and other legal principles, the legal rights and interests of the entire Che family should not be interfered with by any country. However, Che's eldest son, Xi, was suddenly arrested in the French Concession on November 22nd of this year. It is reported that he has been taken to the Japanese consulate and illegally detained. Xi is a member of the Chinese Nationalist Party (Kuomintang), and he is usually law-abiding and is currently studying. He has not participated in any illegal activities. Factually, he is innocent of any arrest. Legally, the French Concession is Chinese territory, and even if there is a place where he should be restrained, it is not the Japanese consulate that can make excuses to arrest him. The Che family has repeatedly presented the permit and politely requested his release, but all have been rejected. This matter concerns Che's individual legal rights. The law firm of Yunmei, Xu Jie, and Luo Zhaoxin is legally negotiating, and Mr. Chen Yang and Mr. Li Shichang have been asked to represent and petition the authorities. In addition, I hope that all national legal organizations and wise people at home and abroad will provide support so that Che's son can regain his freedom. I offer my sincere prayers. Respectfully, Jin Che, December 1st.

Zheng Chengqing's Remarks 112

Yesterday, a reporter from the News Society specially visited Mr. Zheng Chengqing of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to inquire about the details of the Jin case. According to Mr. Zheng, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce received a letter a few days ago requesting the rescue of Jin Xi, along with a photograph of Jin Xi's nationality certificate. There is no doubt that Jin Xi is a citizen of the Republic of China. The French Concession authorities, in violation of the agreement of the French Concession Court, allowed the Japanese to arrest our citizens within the concession, which is truly inappropriate. Therefore, for the sake of national sovereignty, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has petitioned the municipal government to negotiate seriously. Mr. Zheng also showed the photograph of the nationality certificate. The original text of the certificate is recorded below: (Ministry of Interior Nationality Permit No. 67, stating the permitted naturalized person Jin Yongduo, male, age 39, native place Joseon, Jin Nan Hampyeong County, Xinguang Nanham Seungri, residence, Shanghai French Concession, Blanc Niermont Malang Road, 446, those who obtain nationality along with the naturalized person, wife Cui Huichun, age 30, eldest son Jin Xi, age 18, second son Jin Degen, age 16, daughter Jin Meiqing, age 1, the aforementioned Jin Yongduo, applying for permission to naturalize in the Republic of China in accordance with the Nationality Law of the Republic of China, meets the statutory conditions and should be permitted. In addition to registration by the Ministry, a permit is issued. This certificate, October 15th, 18th year of the Republic of China.

Jin Xi is Not the Principal Offender 113

According to Japanese newspapers in Tokyo, Jin Xi, who was captured in Shanghai, is the main culprit in the Hongkou Baichuan case from the previous year. Upon investigation, Jin and his father, Jin Che, were captured by the Japanese the previous winter. Afterwards, Wu Kaisheng and Cai Xiaobai negotiated with the French Consul and finally secured their release. Due to the issue of Chinese traitors, various interactions between Ji Zhuqing and Wu Chengyu, and Jin Xi and Huang Zhanying, have been reported in Shanghai newspapers. This time, he was captured by the Japanese again. The reporter from the News Society specially interviewed Mr. Ji Zhuqing, asking if Jin was as reported in the Tokyo newspapers. Ji said that although they had organized a Sino-Korean anti-Japanese group with Jin, the purpose was to advance and retreat in accordance with the Chinese government's policy towards Japan, and not to carry out any conspiracy in the hope of luck. Unexpectedly, many rumors were fabricated by Chinese traitors and secretly reported to the other side, claiming that the Hongkou case was masterminded by Jin. However, Jin was only 20 years old at the time and could only do propaganda work. Moreover, Jin Jiu had already stepped forward to admit responsibility for the Hongkou case. Even if it was not Jin Jiu, it must have been an important figure in Korea, and Jin Xi could not have participated in it. Last year, because their group was betrayed by unscrupulous elements, the undersigned and Jin Xi and others published announcements withdrawing from the group. Since then, Jin has stopped propaganda work as well. At the beginning of this month, Jin sent a letter asking me to help him find a job. Because I was unable to help, I did not proceed. This letter is still with me, which further proves that Jin's crime is related to the Hongkou case. The Japanese are exaggerating their claims only to expose that they were sold out by Chinese traitors.

No Previous Deficits 114

The city's finances have always been quite ample. Although there has been no surplus each year, there have also been no deficits. Over the years, efforts have been made to rectify various tax revenues. For example, the income in the 16th year of the Republic was only over 3 million, but it increased to over 5 million in the 18th year and over 8 million in the 20th year. Although the income in the 21st year was affected by the January 28th Incident, it was still higher than in previous years. However, after the January 28th Incident, the city's expenditures increased sharply, making it difficult to balance revenue and expenditure. Therefore, increasing revenue and reducing expenditure are currently necessary.

Periodic Land Tax Collection 115

The city's financial situation has indeed felt extremely strained recently. The municipal government has ordered the bureau to quickly seek ways to increase revenue and reduce expenditure. The undersigned (蔡氏自稱, Cai, referring to himself) believes that the land value tax is the proper way to increase revenue, and the concession authorities have already started collecting it. The central government also has regulations on collection. Given the high land prices in the city and the city's financial difficulties, collection is indeed necessary. Therefore, the city has already notified landlords in the urban area to start collecting the second installment of the land value tax for this year from the 21st of this month, and to pay it at designated locations within two months of the start of collection.

Sharp Increase in Security Expenses 116

The reason why the city's finances feel strained is that security expenses after the January 28th Incident increased from 2 million to 3.5 million. Before the January 28th Incident, the city's security expenses, excluding public security fees, were all borne by the central government. However, since the January 28th Incident, the city established a security office. Given the vast area of the city and the mix of people from all over, a stronger security force is needed to maintain order. Therefore, the establishment of the security office was indeed necessary. However, after the establishment of the security office, the city's security expenses increased by more than 1 million. Security expenses have always been offset by income from house rentals. The house rental collected in the city is only about 2.3 million. Now that security expenses have increased to about 3.5 million, the difference is a shortfall of about 1.2 million. This cannot be offset by rectifying the old taxes. Now that the central government has approved the collection of land value tax, which can generate more than 1 million yuan per year, the city's finances may be balanced.

Ministry of Finance Instructs Guohua Bank to Operate With Confidence, Finding that the Bank is Not Related to the Fujian Incident 117

According to the New Voice News, during the January 28th Incident, Shanghai Guohua Bank, along with the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Shanghai Bankers' Association, and the Shanghai Local Coordination Association, were moved by righteous indignation and collected patriotic donations for the 19th Route Army. Therefore, they were feared by the Japanese. After the 19th Route Army's rebellion in Fujian, rumors were spread to undermine the bank. Fearing that the public would misunderstand and affect finance, the bank formally requested the Ministry of Finance for protection. The Ministry of Finance sent officials to investigate in detail. It was found that Deng Ruiren and others had used a business name to deposit more than 50,000 yuan in shares. The 19th Route Army's deposits were withdrawn on November 3rd, leaving no balance. The remittance exchanges of the Xiamen branch were also investigated one by one, and all were purely commercial transactions with no affiliation or aid to the rebellious party. The Ministry of Finance instructed the bank to operate with confidence. The bank's business is as usual. Yesterday, which was Sunday, the bank's four branches in Baxianqiao, Hongkou, Xinzha, and Nanshi were all open at 10 am as usual, with no unusual circumstances.

Representatives of Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Industries Return to Shanghai 122

According to New Voice News, the representatives of the joint association of the Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou tobacco and alcohol industries, Yu Xunlu, Zhang Dalian, Zhang Suhou, Jin Yunjie, Gao Youming, Ru Baiquan, Cao Gexian, Wang Xinpu, and others, have returned to Shanghai after completing their petition in Beijing. According to a statement released by the representatives, the details of the Q&A regarding the revision of the new tobacco and alcohol tax with Gu Aicang, director of the Tax Department of the Ministry of Finance, are as follows: (Question) The tax rates are unfair. (Answer) In the past, the public sales collection fee was 20% of the value of the goods. What is the percentage of the new tobacco and alcohol system? It has not been clearly announced, and merchants have doubts. (1) Shaoxing wine, new system, the production tax is 1.4 yuan, and the sales tax is 2 yuan. According to the previous public sales method, the production and sales each paid half of the tax. The new system actually collects 0.6 yuan. It is requested to reduce the sales tax rate by 0.6 yuan, so that it is equal to the production tax increase. (2) Imitation Shaoxing wine (this wine is a local yellow wine made by Shaoxing merchants in the Soviet Union) has always been taxed the same as local yellow wine because its raw materials are no different and its selling price is similar. Now the new system lists them in two categories. The tax on local yellow wine is 0.8 yuan, and the tax on imitation Shaoxing wine is 1.4 yuan, an increase of 0.6 yuan. It is requested to return it to one category so that it is taxed the same as local yellow wine. (3) Local yellow wine in Shanghai. Shanghai is a special area. The workshops are located in Pudong in the Chinese district. At the beginning of the public sale, there was no tax in the concessions, and tax was levied in the Chinese district, which was clearly discriminatory. Therefore, since the fourth year of the Republic of China, Hong Xiaochu, the director of Dunhou Hall of the industry, requested Xie Weitang, the sub-bureau chief of the Second District Tobacco and Alcohol Affairs Bureau, to submit a request to the provincial bureau to send personnel to investigate and adjust it. A special license (i.e., half-tax license) was issued so that the industry's merchants could pay tax and affix licenses for selling wine to the concessions, while still obtaining full licenses for sales to various ports in the Chinese district. This has been implemented for nearly 20 years. Now, the new system has failed to implement collection in the concessions, and goods are still tax-free. In the Chinese district, the half-tax license has been abolished and full tax has been forced to be levied, making it impossible for the industry's merchants to maintain their business, and they are about to declare closure. It is requested to show compassion and maintain the half-tax license. (Question) What is the situation of extortion along the way? (Answer) In the past, during the public sale period, the production site first reported half of the tax and obtained a waybill. After passing through, the waybill and goods matched and were released unimpeded. Until the sales site, the other half of the tax was reported. Now, however, the production and sales are collected together, and the tax certificate is actually affixed. There are all kinds of difficulties along the way, which are difficult to describe in words. It is only necessary to send personnel for secret investigation to know its numerous abuses. If this continues, how can merchants bear it? It is requested to strictly investigate and punish those who commit crimes to reassure the good. (Question) The penalties are too severe. What is the real situation? (Answer) In the past, the public sale was calculated by jar. Now the new system collects by volume. If the volume per jar is slightly different, it is actually the error of the local tax bureau and not the merchant taking advantage of it to evade tax. Even if strict measures are taken, it is possible to pay the tax according to the scene. Confiscation and punishment are not. It is requested to order the merchant to show compassion and exempt them from confiscation and punishment. (Question) What is meant by resembling double taxation? (Answer) The goods in stock have already paid the public sale fee and tax. Why is it necessary to change the rules and make up for the old and new? As with flour, yarn, matches, cement, etc. in the past, unified tax was levied without retroactive payment. This can be used as clear proof. Moreover, during the public sale period, merchants' goods in stock were established for buying and selling, and taxes were paid and licenses were obtained. Now, goods that have been forced to be manufactured must be taxed and licensed. The number is quite large, and merchants do not have the ability to bear it. The deadline for selling out in six months, the size of the merchant's business cannot be predetermined. After six months, will taxes be paid again? Moreover, the places where the goods are stored are humid, with insects and rats, and rain and wind. It is difficult to preserve the original condition of the affixed certificates, which will inevitably lead to disputes. It is requested to order that stocks be taxed and licensed at the time of sale. (Question) How is the treatment so different? (Answer) The quality of local tobacco leaves varies greatly. The best are smoked tobacco leaves, which can cost 70 to 80 yuan, or 40 to 50 yuan. The lowest are foot skin and autumn tobacco, which cost only 2 to 3 yuan. This kind of planting is for farmers. The new system taxes them all at the same rate of 4.15 yuan, which exceeds the cost and will inevitably cut off planting, affecting rural life and affecting social order. It is requested to classify and set taxes according to local wine to show fairness.

Customs Recovers Pilotage Management Rights, Organizes Pilotage Management Committee, Pilot Trainees Limited to Chinese 129

The right to use pilots at Chinese seaports, since the second article of the General Regulations on Pilotage at Various Seaports stipulated in the seventh year of Tongzhi, stipulates that all Chinese people and nationals of treaty countries who are willing to serve as pilots are allowed to serve equally. However, the right of examination is controlled by the examination bureau jointly organized by the shipping firms and various countries' consuls. Therefore, the number of people involved has become an example of holding a great power. Over the years, the right of successful candidates to serve as pilots in various seaports has disappeared. Navigation rights have been lost invisibly. In order to recover this management right, the government recently placed all pilotage associations in various ports along the river and coast under the jurisdiction of the government. It has also formulated 46 articles of Provisional Regulations on Pilotage Management to replace the previous General Regulations on Pilotage at Various Seaports. The following is about this:

Yesterday's Memorial Service for Mr. Wu Changshuo Attended by Over Two Thousand from Chinese and Foreign Art Circles 130

Mr. Wu Changshuo of Anji, a master of morals, literature, and art, has returned to the immortal realm. Seven weeks have passed since his passing. Chinese and foreign art circles, along with his former students and old friends, initiated a seventh-week memorial. Jueyuan Temple was used as the site for the memorial service and an exhibition of his posthumous works. Yesterday, in addition to the memorial service, associates displayed their artistic talents. Their calligraphy and paintings evoked the movement of dragons and snakes, the engraving of metal and stone seemed to burst into life, and spirits guarded the works at night. The fame of his work spread far and wide. Blessed by the Creator, he was suitable for both old and young. How can we not mourn his passing, which occurred in this inauspicious year? Now, seven weeks have passed. We mourn his absence. His artistic spirit shall endure, and his descendants will carry on his legacy. May this offering be accepted. Besides the memorial service, famous figures from across the country, respected elders from the north and south, as well as European, American, and Japanese artists, attended the public memorial, with the number of attendees reaching around two thousand. The garden and its rocks were serene and beautiful, and the weather was pleasant, making the atmosphere even better. Mr. Wu's posthumous works were displayed in two large rooms upstairs and downstairs, all of which were carefully crafted masterpieces, numbering over a hundred. Some came from the collections of Europeans, Americans, and Japanese, while others came from the collections of his relatives. The walls were adorned with treasures, making it feel like entering a treasure mountain. The portrait of Mr. Wu in the hall was a continuation by Mr. Ren Bonian, with exquisite brushwork and dignified appearance. Mr. Shen Qiquan presided over the memorial service and personally wrote the eulogy, which read, "On the third day of the twelfth month of the twenty-second year of the Republic of China, Shen Wei and others respectfully offer wine, milk, incense, and fruit to the spirit of Mr. Wu of Canlu, saying: O Mr. Wu, your capacity was as vast as the sea and your burden as heavy as the earth. You had world-class ambition, but were confined. Now, freed from restraint, you are paired with the ancients, roaming the coastal areas, with poetry in your heart and wine on your lips." The Japanese also used floral arrangements and matcha tea, and played the flute and music. The ceremony was solemn and grand. Mr. Yamada Kenkichi wrote the eulogy during the memorial. After the service, Buddhist Guan Jiongzhi and a hundred lay Buddhists piously chanted scriptures. The Japanese Buddhist delegation and the monks of Jueyuan Temple all participated, making it a rare grand event in the art world.

Memorial service for Mr. Wu Changshuo (photographed by Ye Changlie)

The details are as follows:

Shanghai Water Administration Commission: According to Article 2 of the Provisional Regulations for Water Administration, the water affairs of Shanghai shall be governed by the Water Administration Commission, which shall be composed of representatives from the following personnel: two representatives from the Ministry of Finance, one representative each from the General Staff Headquarters, the Ministry of the Navy, the Ministry of Transportation, and the local Chamber of Commerce, and one representative from the Harmony Chamber of Commerce.

Members of the Management Committee: Those appointed by Liu Ji include Mr. Hillman, representative of the Ministry of Finance and concurrently Chairman of the Maritime Patrol Works Department, Mr. Green, Port Director, Lin Zixin, representative of the General Staff Headquarters, Xu Jixiang, representative of the Ministry of the Navy, Gao Tingzi, representative of the Ministry of Transportation. Representatives from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Harmony Chamber of Commerce are currently being selected.

Investigation of Water Guiding Organizations in Shanghai: According to the regulations, all water guiding organizations in Shanghai should be governed by the committee. According to the investigation by the Xinsheng News Agency, these organizations include: (1) Songhan Water Guiding Association, (2) Shanghai Lingjiang Company, (3) Wusong Hankou Water Guiding Company, and (4) Japanese Yangtze River Pilot Association.

Powers of the Water Administration Committee: The powers of the Water Administration Committee are summarized as follows: (1) The Water Administration Committee shall, according to the conditions of each port, formulate detailed rules for managing water pilots within its area, divide the water guiding boundaries, stipulate the number of water pilots and water guiding students, and their fees, and submit them to the Ministry of Finance for consultation with the relevant departments. (2) The Water Administration Committee shall be responsible for verifying the employment of qualified water pilots and supervising their professional conduct, as well as the qualifications of water guiding students in each area. If water pilots or water guiding organizations in each area have complaints against others or are accused by others, the Water Administration Committee shall discuss and handle them. (3) The Management Committee of each port shall, according to the number of water pilot quotas, examine and issue water pilot practice certificates to qualified water pilots. (4) When there are not enough qualified water pilots to meet the water pilot quota in each port, the Water Administration Committee shall select experienced Chinese water pilots and grant them practice certificates for probationary employment. (5) The Water Administration Committee may exercise the power to impose disciplinary actions, suspend their business, impose fines, or revoke their practice certificates. Those who are subject to disciplinary action and disagree with the disciplinary judgment may request a review by the competent department, which shall be jointly decided by the Ministry of Finance.

Qualifications for Water Guiding Trainees: The qualifications for water guiding trainees are as follows: (1) Citizens of the Republic of China aged between 25 and 45; (2) Certified by a doctor to be physically and mentally healthy, strong, and without other bad habits; (3) Their vision must be at least 1/9.6, and their color vision must be accurate; (4) Their hearing must be able to distinguish ordinary low voices at a distance of six meters; (6) Familiar with the waterways in the water guiding area and have served as senior officers on ships navigating within the national territorial waters for more than two years; (7) Familiar with the tides in the waterways of the water guiding area and able to calculate the depth of water using tide tables; (8) Familiar with all facilities in the waterways of the water guiding area; (9) Familiar with the ports in the water guiding area and the location of mooring buoys, piers, etc. within the port; (10) Able to read nautical charts, apply the variation of the compass, determine the direction of navigation, and change the course of the ship; (11) Familiar with and able to apply the International Regulations for Preventing Collisions at Sea; (12) Able to perform the duties of piloting ships; (12) Proficient in one foreign language.

The cotton and rice planted in the farmland of various districts of Shanghai County suffered two wind disasters, resulting in damage and poor harvest. Shanghai Municipal Zoo Finalizes Competition Rules for Hibiscus Birds: Over 100 Birds Registered, All Fine Breeds; Judging and Awards Procedures Also Determined 134

The Shanghai Municipal Zoo's first Hibiscus Bird Competition has been finalized and will be held on the 12th of this month in the lecture hall of the Municipal Public Education Center. Currently, 83 bird owners have registered. Although the registration period ended at the end of last month, it is said that good breeds can still be registered. According to Director Shen of the zoo, the birds participating in the competition are temporarily divided into six categories: Chinese, German, Norwegian, Dutch, British, and Mixed. The exact number has not yet been counted, but it is estimated to be about one hundred and several dozen. Each exhibitor is limited to one item per variety. The zoo is currently hiring experts to serve as judges. The judging criteria will be based on body shape and feather color, each accounting for 25%, and song accounting for 50%. For those that do not sing and are only for viewing, feather color will account for 60% and body shape 40%. The three entrants with the highest scores in each group will be awarded certificates. The entrant with the highest overall score in all groups will be awarded a trophy. In addition, the zoo will solicit prizes from various organizations for distribution. The zoo has issued invitations, inviting various organizations and legal entities to attend and provide guidance. Ordinary visitors will be charged an admission fee of one corner to limit entry.

Dredging Bureau Orders the Largest Dredger in the Far East from Germany 135

Song Ziliang, Director of the Dredging Bureau, recently signed a contract with the German shipyard Hegu, represented by the Shanghai Siemens Electric Factory, to manufacture a state-of-the-art suction dredger for dredging the sandbars of the Yangtze River, named "Fairy Flats." This is one of the largest ocean-going dredgers in the world, measuring 360 feet in length, 60 feet in width, and able to dredge to a maximum depth of 45 miles. Its maximum dredging capacity is 18 feet, and its fully loaded sailing speed is 10 and a quarter knots. The machine will be built in the Elbin Shipyard within one year from now. The machine will be transported to Shanghai by automatically sailing from the Suez Canal. It can dredge 35,000 tons of mud per day, sucking the river mud into the machine's bucket and then discharging it into the sea several miles away. The total value of the machine is said to be 2.3 million national currency.

After Increased Donations for Apartments in the French Concession, Apartment Operators Petition to Maintain Original Donations: Trade Association Details Apartment Nature; Taxpayers Association Asks Authorities to Review 138

In the new western district of the French Concession, the number of apartment businesses has been increasing recently. Therefore, the French Municipal Council has created a new donation system for newly opened apartments, similar to that of small hotels. However, the fourteen oldest businesses, including Dahua, Dacheng, Dayi, Xinping, Kyoto, Huadong, Huabei, Dongfang, Tianjin, Wuling, Beijing, Central, Xindu, and Datong, were granted apartment licenses by the French authorities at the time and were recognized as formal apartments. Unexpectedly, because the Central, Datong, and Xindu apartments moved their locations, the investigators reported them as hotel properties. Therefore, since last month, they have been forced to change to hotel donations, which cost more than five times as much. The operators were shocked by the news and believed that they could not afford the huge expenses in this depressed era. If they refused to pay, the authorities would stop supplying water and electricity. Under the threat of water and electricity from the French authorities, the three apartments had to temporarily pay the donations and united with other businesses to continue their struggle. They also publicly elected representatives to petition the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the French Concession, requesting assistance. Chairman Du Yuesheng of the association allowed the apartment industry to detail the nature of apartments and hotels so that they could forward the request to the French authorities for review in order to reach a peaceful solution. The following is a copy of the Shanghai Apartment Trade Association's letter to Chairman Du Yuesheng of the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association: "Respected Chairman Yuesheng, our three apartment buildings were revoked their apartment business licenses by the French Municipal Council and were ordered to pay donations at the rate of hotels. We have already reported the dispute to you in person. Now, we would like to further detail the differences between apartments and hotels. The establishment of apartments was originally for social responsibility and to reduce the burden on travelers. It is roughly the same as the position of public offices and guild halls in various provinces and ports of our country. Since the central government moved its capital to Nanjing, Shanghai has become an important place for people from the guest industry to travel to and from. Moreover, there are more Chinese and foreigners living together and merchants gathering than in other places. Staying in hotels for a long time is constrained by the economy, and staying with relatives and friends is inconvenient. We have taken this into consideration and have chosen a convenient location in the French Concession with a more secluded location to set up apartments. The rent is similar to that of ordinary family landlords in Shanghai. Here are the main points: (1) The travelers who live in the apartments are all visiting relatives and friends, seeking work, or waiting for errands. They have no sufficient travel expenses available. (2) The room fees charged by the apartments are calculated on a monthly basis, which is both long-lasting and economical. If the travel expenses are insufficient, there is still room for sending letters to urge payment. (3) The apartments are free from all luxury items and do not have the furnishings and extravagance of hotels. The burden is naturally reduced, which is convenient for travelers with insufficient travel expenses. It feels like they have been living here for a long time and do not feel like they are guests. The above three points are the differences between apartments and hotels. On March 1, 1931, we requested the French Municipal Council to allow us to treat us equally and collect business taxes with reference to the management methods of boarding houses in various countries. We were approved to collect 2 taels of donation for every 100 taels of silver in rent. We have been in peace for many years. Until March of this year, the three apartments of our colleagues moved from Yuele Lane on Aiduya Road to Daode Lane on Baylor Road due to the landlord's renovation of the house and paid apartment taxes on a monthly basis for as long as three months. Unexpectedly, the French Municipal Council recently issued an emergency order, revoking the licenses of the three apartment buildings and ordering them to pay taxes according to the hotel tax rate, otherwise the water and electricity would be cut off. Our colleagues were unable to resist and had to pay the money in pain in order to maintain business. At a time when all industries in Shanghai are depressed, the French Municipal Council suddenly increased donations, which is not a policy to protect merchants and the people. Therefore, our colleagues respectfully present the facts to you, hoping that you will observe the lower sentiments and fight for a reason with the French Municipal Council to ask them to collect donations according to the original apartment donation regulations in order to care for the difficulties of merchants and maintain business. We are very eager to await your orders. The association has forwarded the letter to the French Municipal Council for review."

Seafeng Flour Company Fire: Manager Xu Hecheng Accused - Shareholders Demand Rights Due to Suspected Embezzlement of Insurance Funds 146

In Xinfu, Haizhou, there is the Seafeng Flour Company, established during the late Qing Dynasty's Guangxu period, with a total capital of 300,000 yuan. Its first manager was Xu Jiuxiang, who managed it for over a decade, and the business was quite prosperous. After Jiuxiang passed away from illness, his younger brother Xu Hecheng took over the position, and there were no complaints. However, in September of this year, the company suddenly suffered a fire. All assets except for the boilers and furnaces were destroyed, resulting in significant losses. Fortunately, the company had fire insurance, and after the incident, received compensation of 115,000 silver dollars, which Xu Hecheng, Zhu Youqin, Bao Zidan, and others received and deposited in the Bank of Communications on Jielu in this city. They also placed a notice in the newspaper to thank the insurance company. At that time, Wang Xiaowu, a shareholder of Seafeng, saw the wording of the advertisement and found it unusually vague, suspecting that they were trying to embezzle the funds. He, in his capacity as a shareholder or auditor, negotiated with Xu, demanding that he hand over all the insurance funds and historical account books for auditing. However, Xu repeatedly evaded the request and was even suspected of absconding with the money. Therefore, in order to protect their rights, they urgently hired lawyers Zhan Jifeng and Zhan Yigang to file a criminal self-accusation against Xu Hecheng, stating that his succession as manager was not approved by all shareholders and was in fact a theft of office. His leasing of the company was also done without shareholder consent. Furthermore, his attempt to embezzle the insurance funds constituted a violation of Article 356 of the Criminal Law for embezzlement and Article 363 for fraud. They requested that he be promptly arrested, punished according to the law, and ordered to repay the share capital of 91,420 silver dollars, as well as statutory interest. The plaintiff also feared that Xu Hecheng would withdraw the funds deposited in the Bank of Communications, so they specifically requested the court to issue an order to the bank to prohibit Xu Hecheng, Zhu Youqin, Bao Zidan, and others from spending the funds before the case was concluded, in order to protect their claims. The other day, Judge Zhan Liangce of the First Special District Court held a hearing to summon the defendant Xu Hecheng for questioning. Xu Hecheng stated that he was elected as a liquidator by the board of directors in 1918, so he handled the company's lease and received the insurance compensation according to his authority, and it was not an unauthorized action. However, the plaintiff claimed that the defendant's liquidation duties were for clearing his brother's debts and that he was not actually elected by the shareholders. After mutual arguments, Judge Zhan ruled that the case was of great importance and beyond the jurisdiction of the lower court, and ordered it to be transferred to the local court for scheduled trial.

Robbery on Xizang Road Yesterday Morning: Robbers Flee into the Chinese Area, Three Policemen Shot - None of the Six Robbers Captured - Three Policemen Unable to Intercept Due to Isolation - Zhang Dakui's Injury is Critical and Life-Threatening 152

Yesterday morning at around 8:00 AM, a robbery occurred on Xizang Road in the Public Concession. Afterwards, the robbers, fearing pursuit, retreated into Minbei and shot and injured three policemen. The details are as follows:

Six Robbers Arrive 153

Zhou Bocun, a local resident, lives in the east wing of No. 4, Lane 55 (Huatongfang) on Xizang Road in the Public Concession. He works as an accountant in the Shunfeng Securities Company at No. 11, Tong'an Lane, Hankou Road. Because of the proximity to the exchange, Zhou also privately engaged in government bond trading. Over the years, he has accumulated some wealth, which attracted the attention of robbers. Yesterday morning, at around 7:00 AM, Zhou was still in bed due to the Sunday holiday when six robbers suddenly arrived outside his door. Four of them carried handguns, and two stood guard at the front and back doors. One robber guarded the door of the east wing, while the other three, also armed, broke into Zhou's bedroom, woke up everyone in the house, drove them to a corner, and held them captive. They said to Zhou, "Recently, you have been making a lot of money selling government bonds, so we have come to borrow some. Hand over the money quickly, or these guns are merciless." Seeing the situation, Zhou argued with them, but the robbers were aggressive and would not listen. Zhou Bocun had no choice but to hand over the keys and let them search.

Shouting for Robbers from Upstairs 154

After obtaining the keys, the robbers opened the dressing table and drawers in the room. They found 20 silver dollars in cash and a gold ring worth 23 dollars, which they immediately took. Then, seeing that there was nothing else of value, they forced Zhou to hand over the keys to the chests. While they were arguing, the robber guarding the people in the room relaxed his vigilance slightly. Zhou's maid saw an opportunity and escaped, running to the second landlord's attic in the back, waking up the second landlord Pan Xianting and his wife. They reported the robbery. Upon hearing this, Pan and his wife hurriedly got out of bed, closed the door tightly, pushed open the window facing the street, blew the whistle wildly, and shouted for help to catch the robbers. The robbers, hearing this, knew that they had been exposed and were extremely frightened. They quickly turned around, went downstairs, and fled towards the front door. However, nearby police officers patrolling the area near Xizang Road had also been alerted and gathered. Seeing this, the robbers, fearing arrest, quickly turned around, crossed the bridge, and fled towards the Guoqing Road area in the Chinese territory.

Shooting Along the Way 155

Seeing this, the Chinese police officers in the Public Concession, fearing that the robbers would escape, quickly blew their whistles to notify the police officers in the Chinese territory to cooperate in the pursuit. At that time, Zhang Dakui, police officer No. 23 from the Fourth District Police Station at the intersection of Guqing Road and Wuzhen Road, happened to be on duty. He first heard the alarm, and then saw five or six people running towards Wuzhen Road, realizing that they were not good people. He quickly raised his gun and ordered them to stop. However, the robbers had already noticed him and opened fire on Police Officer Zhang first. Zhang's thigh was hit, and the bullet entered his abdomen but did not exit. At the time, the police officer did not realize it and continued to pursue them relentlessly, until he reached the vicinity of Yangzheng Beili on Manzhou Road, where he collapsed due to excessive bleeding. Seeing that they had caused trouble, the robbers quickly turned west and fled into Dunmu Lane. One of the robbers, because he was wearing a long gown, found it difficult to run and took off his Zhigong woolen camel hair gown and abandoned it at the entrance of the lane to escape. This was seen by Zhou Peixin, police officer No. 24 stationed nearby, who quickly fired a shot, intending to arrest him. However, he was also shot by the robber, the bullet hitting his right abdomen and exiting from his back, causing him to fall to the ground with serious injuries.

Bullets Flying 156

Seeing that they had caused two incidents in a row, the robbers became panicked and fled out of Dunmu Lane in a hurry, hiding near the Rice Merchant Association. However, this was also the post of Police Officer Liu Qingren, No. 25, who was already lying in wait. Therefore, a fierce battle broke out between the police and the robbers, with bullets flying and pedestrians fleeing. However, the number of the robbers was few, and there was no support. Therefore, before long, Police Officer Liu was shot down again, the bullet entering his right waist and exiting from his rear thigh. The robbers were able to escape and fled in different directions on North Xinmin Road, without being apprehended. By the time the Chinese police officers from the Public Concession arrived, the robbers had already fled far away. After the Fourth District Headquarters heard the alarm, they quickly dispatched a large number of armed police officers. The fire rescue ambulance dispatched by the concession had arrived earlier and had already rushed the three injured policemen to the Baolong Hospital on Baker Road for treatment. Soon after, Detectives Tang En and Qiu Jingfan from the Huishi Police Station personally went to the scene of the incident to investigate and brought back the long gown abandoned by the robbers and several shell casings found at the scene to the police station for filing. They dispatched detectives to pursue the robbers everywhere. Among the injured police officers, Zhang Dakui's situation was the most critical. Zhang is from Shandong and is 31 years old. Zhou Peixin is from Nanjing and is 32 years old. Liu Qingren is 24 years old and from Shandong. Although the injuries of these two are not minor, their lives can be saved.

(41 years old), Jiang Yitao, (18 years old), Shen Dishan, (28 years old), the female gangster Wang Shenshi, 38 years old, who is the wife of the fugitive mastermind Wang Jintao, and Shen Shenshi, (59 years old), were all arrested and taken to the Sixth District Police Station for questioning separately. Tragic Incident of Killing Son in the Western District of Shanghai - Ma Mengzhou Stabs His Son with a Gun - Ma Fuxin Confesses It Was His Father 157

Ma Mengzhou, a local resident of Shanghai, 49 years old, residing at No. 19, Majiajiao, Hongqiao Road, Western District of Shanghai, is a farmer. He is usually diligent and thrifty, so his family is quite well-off. His wife, Tang, has three sons. The eldest, Fuxin, is 25 years old, born to his first wife, Wang. He used to typeset at a printing house and is married to a woman named Zhang. The second son, Fuxiang, is 22 years old. The youngest, Fuhong, is 14 years old. Mengzhou has an elderly father, Zhonghuan, who is over seventy years old and in good spirits. The family is harmonious. However, Fuxin does not work properly and has become depraved. He has secretly mortgaged the family property and squandered it all, so Mengzhou and his wife hate him deeply. In January of this year, they sent Fuxin to the Caohejing Work Training Center for vagrants and imprisoned him for six months. He was released only last month, but Fuxin still does not repent and associates with rogues, which aroused Mengzhou's intention to kill his son. Moreover, Tang strongly encouraged him. Therefore, at around 8:00 PM the night before, Mengzhou, carrying a very sharp ancient-style long gun, waited on the side of the road opposite Mengjiangtang on Hopeland Road. Before long, Fuxin staggered along, drunk and disoriented. Mengzhou, taking him by surprise, raised the gun and stabbed Fuxin directly in the heart, stabbing him three times. Two of the stabs were in the chest, about an inch deep. The last stab was in the shoulder. Because the gun head fell off, it only slightly broke the skin. Seeing that the attacker was his father, Fuxin jumped into the river beside the road and shouted for help. Mengzhou then fled with the gun pole. At this time, Zeng Shipu, the chief of the Wangjialou Police Station, was patrolling and heard the shout. He went to the scene and rescued Ma Fuxin. He also picked up a handleless sharp gun about eight inches long, stained with blood, on the ground and brought it back to the station. After Chief Zeng questioned him about who the attacker was and how he was attacked, Ma Fuxin initially refused to tell the truth. After repeated strict questioning, he finally revealed that the attacker was his father, Ma Mengzhou. After obtaining the confession, the chief, seeing that the injuries were very serious, sent him to the Red Cross Hospital on Hague Road by car for treatment. He also arrested the attacker, Ma Mengzhou, along with the murder weapon, and sent them to the First Branch of the Sixth District in Beixinjing, and then transferred them to the City Public Security Bureau for interrogation, etc.

Chen Ronggui Died After Being Hit by Wood, Leaving His Family Destitute - His Wife Died of Worry and Grief - The Jiatai Tea Shop Was Sued by the Family - Claiming 50,000 Yuan in Damages for Causing Death by Negligence 158

Chen Ronggui, a Suzhou native residing at Tianlu Shoe Store, 126 Old School Field in the city, worked at the Miye Foreign Firm on Guangdong Road. On May 12 of this year, at around 5:00 PM, he was returning home from work. When he passed by No. 6, Diandang Street in the French Concession, which is the back door of the Old Jiatai Tea Shop on Old North Gate Avenue, a piece of wood fell from the tea shop's three-story drying platform and hit him on the head. He died despite medical treatment, leaving behind his elderly mother, Chen Zhangshi (blind in both eyes), his widowed wife, Huang, five children, and his unmarried sister who remained chaste. The entire family was left with no means of support. Chen's widow, Chen Huangshi, hired a lawyer to file a criminal self-accusation with the Second Special District Court, accusing the owner of the Old Jiatai Tea Shop, Pan Jucai, and the manager, Ye Jishan, of causing death by negligence. In addition to requesting an investigation, she also filed a civil lawsuit seeking 50,000 yuan in damages. The case was repeatedly summoned but not concluded. Chen's wife, Huang, the plaintiff, died of worry and grief in August. Chen's elderly mother, Chen Zhangshi, then hired a lawyer to file a motion with the court to participate. The details of the court hearing have been reported in previous newspapers. After the case was tried, the defendants were found not guilty. Because the plaintiff's side disagreed with the original verdict, they filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The High Court accepted the appeal and, the other day at 4:00 PM, Court President Guo Dezhang, along with Judges Fan and Li, and Prosecutor Zhang, specially opened the Third Criminal Court to hear the case. Both parties attended with their lawyers, and Wang Licheng, the police detective who handled the case, was summoned to testify about the details of the investigation. The lawyers for both parties argued fiercely for the benefit of their clients. After the hearing lasted until about 6:00 PM, the court announced the end of the debate and adjourned to schedule a date for the verdict.

Prince Singh of Nepal, in response to the banquet hosted by Special Envoy Zhang Ming earlier, paid a return visit to Special Envoy Zhang yesterday to express his gratitude. Another Perpetrator, Chen Xiaobiao, Apprehended in the Yan Azhang Murder Case 160

Yan Azhang (also known as Li Azhang), a native of Ningbo, was close friends with a fellow villager named A Hua. Azhang had a handgun that was borrowed for robbery, and the proceeds were spent. Later, when he asked for it back, they quarreled. Azhang planned to secretly report the robbery to the police. A Hua found out about this and hatched a malicious plan. On the evening of August 22, at around 9:00 PM, he, along with Xiang Xiasheng, Chen Qinxi, Zhang Quan, and Xiaobiao, tricked him into going to a remote place on Guiyang Road. A Hua then shot Azhang in a vital spot with the gun, causing him to fall to the ground. Zhang Quan and Chen Qinxi then stripped him of his pants and pushed him into a nearby creek. He was later found by detectives from the Yangshupu Police Station, who pulled him up and sent him to the hospital, where he died despite treatment. Xiang Xiasheng and Chen Qinxi were arrested one after another and sent to the First Special District Court. Xiang was sentenced to three years in prison, and Chen was sentenced to life imprisonment. The details have been reported in this newspaper. The other day, detectives Jin Wanrong and Su Changsheng from the Yulin Road Police Station found out that Chen Xiaobiao was hiding at No. 35, Renxing Street, Yangshupu Road. They secretly went to the address and arrested him. He was identified as 25 years old, from Shaoxing, and taken to the police station for detention. The next morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court. Zhang Tianyin, the lawyer for the police station, stated the previous circumstances and said that the defendant initially denied that his name was Xiaobiao, saying that it was Chen Xilin. However, a cook from the Shanghai Third Yarn Factory identified him as Xiaobiao, and he finally admitted his guilt. He also admitted that Chen Qinxi and Zhang Quan had come to his house three times to ask him to join. He previously lived at No. 523 in the factory's workshop. He said that he could not bring the other two convicted criminals, Xiang and Chen, to court today and requested a postponement. When questioned, Chen Xiaobiao confessed that he knew the deceased Azhang and Chen Qinxi and Zhang Quan. Zhang Quan had brought a handgun to his house to keep it temporarily and asked him to help kill Azhang. At that time, Chen Qinxi refused. Later, Ruo Gong came three times, and he agreed in a moment of confusion. He walked with Azhang and others to the scene of the incident and suddenly heard a gunshot, but he did not know who fired it. The rest of his statement was evasive. Judge Liu Yugui ordered him to be remanded in custody and scheduled a new hearing.

She truly deserves to be called a doctor with a benevolent heart and benevolent skills.

Commentary

Wedding Hazing and Toasting Cigarettes 188

— Qiao

Despite claims that marriage has become civilized, many traditional customs and etiquette persist.

When a new bride arrives at the bridal chamber, relatives and friends must engage in lively and boisterous hazing. As the old saying goes, "For the first three days, there's no seniority; even grandfathers can jump on the bed like tigers." Hazing is considered an essential part of enjoying a wedding feast. In the past, examining the bride's bound feet was a common activity. Now, with the revolution, asking the bride to sing "Drizzling Rain" and shake hands with the groom is considered progress, perhaps? The host of the wedding faces a dilemma: if there is no hazing, it seems too quiet and dull. Another old saying states, "Hazing brings prosperity." There's a bit of philosophy in the idea that prosperity follows hazing. However, if the hazing becomes too aggressive, it's awkward to step in and stop it. Consequently, humorous incidents often occur. It seems that not long ago, a bloody incident resulted from excessive hazing in Xuzhou.

The people of Suzhou, after all, are more relaxed. They always use the excuse of asking for "lucky fruits," tying all conditions to these fruits. If the wedding guests are clever and the bridesmaids are adaptable, generously distributing the lucky fruits and responding with smooth and tactful answers, major issues can be turned into minor ones, and minor ones into nothing at all. The safety of the bridal chamber can be maintained. Therefore, selecting bridesmaids has become an important matter when marrying off a daughter.

Since the male side's well-wishers have created such a chaotic atmosphere for the bride, the female side's well-wishers cannot show weakness. Thus, when the bride returns to her family home, they seize the opportunity to retaliate by toasting the groom repeatedly. If the groom has a soft tongue, he simply cannot cope. Some even learn to kneel and offer wine like Gao Lishi, enduring more than they can bear, yet feeling uneasy about rejecting it. It's more difficult than anything. If the new guests (it's a miracle if a female guest accompanies the groom at the banquet) are skilled in rhetoric or can drink a little on his behalf, it's easier to defuse the situation. However, according to Suzhou custom, the groom cannot leave before the guests have dispersed. Therefore, there are humorous stories of hazing that lasts until dawn, with the groom becoming so drunk that he loses consciousness.

I'm only speaking from the perspective of Suzhou; I don't know how it is elsewhere, but it's likely even more lively than Suzhou. In my opinion, everything should be moderate and not excessive. Both wedding hazing and toasting can add interest and inject a bit of liveliness into the solemn wedding ceremony. If taken too seriously, it can become disappointing and dull.

Rice Bowl 189

— Feng Moni

During my free time each day, I often help out at the tobacco and paper shop downstairs run by a friend, selling cigarettes, which I find quite interesting and a way to pass the time. However, every day there are always a few beggars who come to ask for cigarette boxes. At first, I didn't quite understand why they wanted the cigarette boxes. Later, when they came to ask for them, I asked them what they were used for. They replied: "We want cigarette boxes to use as rice bowls, so we come to bother you every day, sir." After hearing their words, I finally understood that using cigarette boxes as rice bowls meant they were truly destitute.

Eating is indeed a very complex matter, but the rice bowl used for eating is also not easy to obtain. In wealthy families, rice bowls are naturally not a problem. Gilt-edged rice bowls and silver-flowered rice bowls can be chosen at will. Occasionally, they are displeased with a coarse ceramic rice bowl and cannot even swallow the rice, so they scold the servants and replace it with a more elaborate bowl. There are many people like this. Having money, of course, one must put on airs; otherwise, it wouldn't be enough to show off their young master's temperament. For a person to eat, a rice bowl is naturally indispensable, but why be so particular about it? It is the rice that is being eaten, not the bowl. As for being unable to eat the rice when using a coarse rice bowl, it is truly a ridiculous and absurd story, and it is also a demonstration of the inferior character of Chinese young masters. If wealthy young masters were invited to take a stroll through a slum, they would certainly shake their heads in astonishment and say: "Why is hygiene not emphasized here? They eat with those blackish-gray blue-and-white bowls. It's such a strange thing."

Even wealthy people who use gilt-edged rice bowls still distinguish between the quality of the ceramics, while beggars cannot even afford coarse rice bowls and use cigarette boxes instead. Comparing the two is like comparing heaven and hell. Although everyone's circumstances are different, they should be deeply aware of the plight of the poor and should not put on such airs. A person may be wealthy in this lifetime, but if circumstances change one day, then everything will feel unsatisfactory. Therefore, wealthy people have delicacies such as bird's nest and sea cucumber, but only eat half a bowl of rice, either frowning and saying they have no appetite or pressing their chest and saying they have chest pain. Beggars eat the leftovers and scraps of others and still survive with vitality, and they never worry about hygiene or have illnesses like lack of appetite or chest pain. Perhaps the physical constitution of these two types of people is different?

Yellow Hollyhock Storage Method 190

— Tianxu Wosheng

The most reliable method of storage is to first wash the mud off, crush it, and without drying, pack it into kerosene cans. Each can should hold twenty-five catties, and every four cans make one dan. Then, pour "aldehyde solution" (i.e., formaldehyde) into the gaps to completely immerse it. Then seal it with solder. It can be stored until the following year, but do not let air leak out; it will never spoil.

Aldehyde solution is also known as "one-carbon intermediate liquid," translated as "Formalin." A pure product only needs one percent to preserve for more than six months. However, the "Formalin" sold on the market contains only about 40 percent formaldehyde (CH20), and the rest is (H2O), ordinary water, which does not contain carbon gas. Therefore, it needs to be used with four percent, that is, one pound of "Formalin" should be mixed with twenty-five pounds of water to preserve it until the following year without spoiling. Formalin is sold in various instrument shops, but the price listed in the price list is two dollars and fifty cents per pound. If you buy it from industrial raw material stores, the price is cheaper, but it must be in the original barrel. Retail purchases are about eighty cents or one dollar. If there is no place to buy it, you can buy it from the pulp factory, then ten pounds and five pounds can be used, each dan of hollyhock root only uses one pound.

(Note) The soil must be washed clean. If it is not washed clean, the leaching liquid will have black spots that cannot be removed and cannot be used by paper mills.

This year, because growers are devaluing themselves and selling cheaply, each dan has fallen from six yuan to three yuan. However, users are stored in cellars and cannot buy a year's worth of goods at one time. It is estimated that by February and March of next year, they will all complain and switch to using sorghum flowers. If hollyhock roots can be bought, and if it sells for five or six yuan per dan, which is cheaper than sorghum flowers, they will of course still use hollyhock roots. It is possible to set a price limit, register the number of dan with the utilization plant, and introduce it to users at any time, so that both supply and demand can be facilitated, and the unhealthy wind of competition can be avoided, so as not to kill each other.

Record of Parting with Autumn at Tianchi (Part 2) 191

— Zhang Qianjiu

Descending further, we ascended another peak. A huge rock resembled a drum, hence the name Stone Drum Peak. The gazetteer states: "When the drum sounds, it signifies a year of misfortune." Alas, we have not heard the drum sound for a long time. Is this truly a peaceful and prosperous age? On the drum, there is another enormous rock, wide at the top and narrow at the bottom, with its peak extending more than ten feet beyond its base, reaching a height of about a hundred feet. Looking up, one could lose one's hat; viewed from the side, it resembled a frog raising its head, hence the name Frog Peak. The size of the frog gives an idea of the size of the Stone Drum. Returning to the temple gate via the old path, the so-called Tianchi had already been spoiled by Yi Jun's search for obstructions. The lotus flowers were now gone, leaving only duckweed. Ni Jun and Lan Jun took photos beside it, while Fen Jun stood silently with her head bowed, as if in thought. Ning Jun said, "We've already taken the tour, what's there to think about?" She happily waded barefoot into Tianchi, youthful exuberance captured in a photo. At that time, the autumn sun was still in the mountains, but dusk was deepening. We returned to the boat along the original route, the evening glow on our oars painting a particularly desolate scene of autumn. I believe that the beauty of Tianchi lies solely in its stones, and the beauty of its stones is unmatched elsewhere. Therefore, I record a chapter of Yuan Gu Zhongying's poem "Traveling to Tianchi" as its epilogue:

Winding white cloud path,

Elegant green mountains linked.

Autumn wind blows travelers' robes,

Free spirit fluttering.

Grasping vines, crossing sheer cliffs,

Stepping on stairs, reaching the highest peak.

Cliffs tilting, stones about to fall,

Trees broken, clouds reconnecting.

Two peaks gnawing at each other's gates,

What vastness within the valley!

Great mountains towering,

Almost scraping the blue sky.

Small mountains also rugged,

Flying along in front.

Darkly accumulating ancient iron,

Brightly blooming blue lotus.

Divine axe carving emerald bones,

Heavenly pond holding spiritual spring.

Jade dragon embraces a cold mirror,

Reflected clear autumn hangs.

Remember Zhang Zhenju of old,

Sent me a dazzling poem.

The past cannot be made again,

New poems tied as a tradition.

Raise wine to toast the white sun,

Ten thousand valleys give birth to desolate smoke.

Hidden joy bitterly insufficient,

Sunset suddenly moves.

Why do the beauties not come?

Mountains and waters empty and beautiful.
