Modern Celebrity Calligraphy and Painting 258

Red Silk Embroidered Handkerchief Rambling with Love

I Would Rather Marry You Than Precious Niang

A Message to the Scholars of the Eastern Neighborhood

This Song is Accomplished in a Forest of Green Leaves

Zhen Jiu's Work at Hongdou Pavilion Tan Yunshan

— Tan Yunshan's Calligraphy

To seek wealth and obtain wealth, to get whatever one wants, isn't that delightful? But there are also two things to avoid most when asking for help, which must also be known. The first point is, if the important person you are asking for help from used to be humble, and you once helped or promoted him, be sure not to bring up old things. You think you are expressing kindness and inspiring his conscience, but you don't know that important people value face most and are most afraid of exposing their past shortcomings. If you must speak out, he will be ashamed and angry at that time, turn his face, and will definitely repay kindness with hatred. The second point is, if the important person you are asking for help from puts on airs and gives you a big lecture, be sure not to be unable to bear it, you must be calm, smile, and sincerely accept the lesson. This is a good opportunity to show your flattery, don't miss it. Moreover, since you are asking for help, the fact is that you need him to be a tool for you to find a job, like a farmer needing an ox, or a rider needing a horse. If you think like this, you will definitely be calm and not get angry or talk about integrity.

Relying on Oneself 259

— Local

After returning from the printing press with the proofs, it was already past ten o'clock. Treading on the brick road under the hazy moonlight and dim starlight, the shadows of the trees flickered! The spirit in my mind was suddenly attacked by terrifying thoughts, transforming into a hideous ghost! The strings of my heart suddenly felt terrified! Trembling! I quickened my pace, hoping to leave the dark and terrifying world as soon as possible.

In the defeated yellow weeds, the small insects were emitting miserable wails! They were begging for help, they were asking for, begging for the aid of people, asking for the sympathy of people. The current late autumn, being crushed by the giant wheel of the times, is about to disappear. The cold and windy winter night will soon begin to wreak havoc. Little insects! How do you feel about the bone-piercing winter, how will you get through it?

Nature is giving them cruel coercion! How will they resist it? They are sad! They are afraid! Exhausting their strength, they sing a desperate lament! Ah, little insects! It is a mistake for you to beg for mercy from the people on this night road! Do you know? In this cold and biting autumn night, when the noble people, they have long closed their doors tightly, burrowed into their warm quilts, and are making their sweet dreams. Those who are not afraid of the cold wind and dew and are walking on the road! Like me! They are all like you! Little insects! Laborers who are suffering the same fate! I will tell you, their environment, their surroundings, are just as miserable and pitiful as yours. How can a single piece of clothing covering their bodies resist the violence of nature? How will they get through the cold winter? Therefore, they also deeply feel sad and afraid, but in order to cover up with a false mask of shame, they do not, like you, cry out in a voice hoarse with exhaustion?

Because of this, your begging for help should still be directed to the rich and noble gentlemen! But, the hearts of the gentlemen are all made of iron! They are not even willing to help the poor who are on the same line, the same kind, so where will they find the sympathy to sympathize with you! Therefore, in my opinion, your hope of asking them is slim, there is no possibility of realization, or like me, hold on to the principle of "relying on oneself"! Little insects, get up quickly, fight, seek your survival, if you still do not realize the truth until death, and still beg for help from others, and wail, then, in the end, the only thing you can do is to stretch your neck and submit to the execution!

Fifteen minutes later, I ran into the dormitory, lit the lights, and finally temporarily escaped from this dark world. But the current brightness is so false! The darkness of the past will be born again in an instant.

Written in the dormitory on the 28th of November.

The Child's Mischief 260

— Meng Yuan

In the evening, after eating dinner and chatting for a while, Bin, like a yuanbao, hugged his four-year-old son, Zigang, and said:

"Good boy! Good boy! Today you will go to sleep with grandma; there are delicious things on grandma's bedside; go ahead; grandma is waiting for you to eat!" Bin seemed to be murmuring a prayer.

But the child shouted, "I won't go, I want to stay with Mom tonight."

Bin frowned and looked at Ling with a bitter face.

"What to do? This child is so stubborn!"

His wife sat aside with a smiling face, watching Bin's anxious expression, and couldn't help but smile and glance at him. Bin patted Zigang's back and coaxed him, saying:

"Go ahead! Good boy! Grandma is calling you! You used to sleep with grandma for a few days, and grandma was very happy with you; if you don't go, grandma won't love you anymore!"

"A'nan, go ahead! Your dad is getting anxious!" Ling said in a teasing and understated tone.

"I won't go, I won't go, I want Mom..." The child was still making trouble, shouting, and his two small hands were slapping and hitting Bin's face.

"This little guy, he doesn't know what's good for him!" Bin was furious! He blamed the child and threw him onto the sofa, so the child started to cry loudly!

After letting go, he regretted being too reckless! Bin glanced at Ling's face, only to see her say with a cold face:

"Why don't you just throw him to his death? Then you'll be quiet: I know you don't need children!"

"What a joke, look how hateful this child is! I tried every possible way to coax and please him, but he still wants to make trouble like this?..."

"Hum! Coaxing and pleasing, you only care about your own happiness, and don't care about my child!"

"What a joke! Isn't he my child too?"

"Then why do you treat her like this?"

"Okay! I admit I was wrong...okay..."

Ling pouted and ignored him, ran to the sofa, and picked up Zigang:

"A'nan! Don't cry, listen to Mom, go to sleep with grandma today; tomorrow Mom will buy you a small toy gun to play with."

"I also want a small horse." The child laughed!

The matter of the day dissipated like smoke; the child was taken to grandma's foreign-style house by Bin as usual. When he came back, he saw his wife folding the quilt. She turned her face and said:

"Look at your own stubborn nature, and you still blame the child for being stubborn and making trouble: How come he was willing to go obediently as soon as I came?..." As she said, she pursed her lips and smiled. Bin also laughed.

The Tears of a Clown 261

— Yi Ping

Plato said: "Human society is a big stage." We only look at the smiling faces on the front stage every day, but we don't understand the various things behind the scenes. The comedy that artists perform on stage? It is the whole of life. If we uncover the background behind the scenes, there are material slaves and oppressed tears. Look, that clown, dressed in a painted face, runs out from behind the stage to be made fun of by the audience. He is always wearing a smile, or perhaps it is when his tears have not yet dried. We have seen Lang Que Nai's Langh Crown Langh and Emil Jannings' Blue Angel, so Chekhov told us: "Our compatriots are crawling out of various different holes."

Let me explain the back of the stage to you. The role of the clown is below all roles. He is hired to put on a painted face to reconcile the audience's mood before the main role appears. He shouts, dances, and tells various stories that can elicit a smile from people. If the audience laughs, he can win the favor of the troupe leader, so he is always wearing a smile. The fate of his parents, wife, and children is completely tied to his smiling face. Within the laughter, behind the smiling face, who knows that it is the crystallization of tears?

There was a famous clown in Europe. Because he wanted to study the art of clowning, he forgot the obligations he should fulfill to his wife, but his wife could not forgive him because she was also a clown who wanted to win the favor of the audience and the troupe leader. His life was to seek survival on a smiling face. Finally, while he was wearing a painted face and laughing, his wife left a letter and ran away; however, this poor clown, no matter how painful he was and how desperate he was to shed tears, he always wore a smiling face on the front stage. Do you want to see the tears of a clown? Please go to the backstage.

The sound of unemployment is filling our ears in China. Recently, the deaths of two clowns have uncovered the backstage. It turns out that they have a solid position in the scope of their profession. They jump and shout every day to win the favor of the audience and the troupe leader. However, one died without funeral expenses, and the other committed suicide due to the pressure of life. We see their smiling faces on the front stage every day, but the backstage is filled with tears behind the scenes?

"Human society is a big stage." The background of the clown has been revealed, but on this big stage, there are also our compatriots who are wearing smiling faces and want to win the favor of the audience and the troupe leader, but without success. Crawl out of various holes and come to this big stage to play a clown who is always wearing a smiling face.

Wife's Misunderstanding 262

— Meng Yuan

Cui was my wife Li's classmate, and they were also very good friends.

Before I talked about love with Li, I had a few love songs with Cui first; but in the end, my friendship with Cui faded! Then I became Li's only prisoner. So my process with Cui was an open secret in front of Li. Sometimes when I said that Cui had some shortcomings, my wife would often tease me in a playful tone, saying, "Your Cui is the best!" But Li's friendship with Cui still maintained a normal state.

Unexpectedly, there was an exception! I praised Cui a few words unintentionally, which aroused "my wife's lesson." This was about half a month ago, and I wrote about it in this publication on the 28th of last month.

Now let's recall a past event; this was probably in the spring of this year:

My wife was feeling unwell and fell ill! After I sent her to the train station to return to her hometown to recuperate, it was quite lonely, especially on Sundays! Sometimes I could still bear it and sit at home alone to write manuscripts; but this loneliness could not leave my heart after all, and I was even more worried about my wife's illness, and I was even more depressed! So, the decadent mood could only be spent in places where money was spent.

Of course, it was also a very lonely and depressing Sunday afternoon when I accidentally ran into Cui and two of Cui's girlfriends at the Nanjing Grand Theater. The door of the ticket office was so crowded that Cui smiled at me and then frowned; so I volunteered to squeeze into the crowd and bought four tickets, and we sat down together.

Before the show started, Cui gently asked me:

"Why didn't Li come with you?"

"Because she is unwell, she went to the countryside last week to recuperate!"

"What? Li is sick! Why didn't we good sisters tell us?"

Afterwards, the intense and exciting action on the screen stopped our conversation; at the end of the show, everyone said goodbye and left!

After returning home, I planned to tell my wife about meeting Cui in a letter; but after a second thought, I thought it was unnecessary to do so! Maybe my wife would say to me, "You are always so concerned about Cui's affairs." So, I only told my wife that I watched a movie in Nanjing, but I didn't mention meeting Cui.

Four or five days later, my wife's reply came! It started by saying:

"Yuan:

Why do you always like not to let me know about some things? Haven't you and Cui's affairs been

Page 20

Page 21

Open to me? I deeply feel your pure and sincere love for me, and I also understand your frankness; but, Yuan, can you let me know everything about you? Isn't this your purest and most frank expression? But, Yuan! Why are you unwilling to tell me about some things? Yesterday I received a letter from Cui, she said: Thank you for inviting her to watch a movie, and also asked me if I was feeling well?..."

After I finished reading the letter, I felt ashamed and couldn't help but regret it: It wasn't that I regretted inviting Cui to watch a movie, it was that I blamed myself for being too mindful! Why didn't I tell my wife frankly? "I suffered myself by having a guilty conscience." Damn, damn! This time, my dear wife doesn't know how much trouble she will have?

That night, I spent two hours writing four pages of manuscripts, carefully explaining it to my wife in a tactful way, in order to seek her understanding.

Not many days later, my wife's letter came. I hurriedly took it out and finished reading it in one breath, so the matter was put down like a heavy stone of a thousand pounds, and things were much easier!

A Newspaper Reader in a Mansion 263

— Jian Ping

When the master opened his eyes every morning, he didn't even have time to eat white fungus before he hurriedly flipped through the daily business news: it is said that his whole day's joys and sorrows were completely tied to this moment.

Because the mistress didn't know many characters, she only looked at the advertisements of the three companies and the discount news of Xulun Datonghang.

The concubine was a famous movie fan and theater fan, so after her various daily tasks such as applying rouge and powder, drawing eyebrows, and manicuring her nails, she must carefully check the movie advertisements and stage advertisements to determine her whereabouts for the day.

The young master originally liked to look at the local news, and he was not willing to easily let go of any news about jealousy, rape, abduction, and escape, especially the dog races three times a week.

But recently, he has been paying attention to the classified advertisements for renting and transferring, and it is said that he is now eager to arrange a "golden house" to fulfill his long-cherished wish of "hiding a beauty"!

The young lady's habit of reading the newspaper was very similar to that of the mistress, but she also knew some movie advertisements and dance hall news.

Aguan usually only flipped through cartoons and illustrations, but since a group of imported circuses came, it aroused a lot of his interest.

As for the dry and tasteless party and government news and the irrelevant diplomatic policies, no one wanted to look at them at all. Even the things that our fellow journalists considered to be the crystallization of their brains only got a false title of "something" to hide away; if they were lucky, they might still be able to find a "fragment" on the pancake and fried dough stick stall in the future.

Novel

Shanghai (10) 264

— Zhang Lao San

I escaped from the countryside, thinking that Shanghai could always accommodate me; but within two days, Shanghai gave me too much disappointment. Like my sister Min, that companion who sympathized with me, ran to the paradise of heaven. Uncle, just bring the things here faintly. My cousin, the urban girl, seems to be deeply in love with me. The courage that I barely mustered, from the countryside to Shanghai, from Shanghai to the hotel, from the foreign villa to the tram, has disappeared without a trace. Go back, I can never leave my younger brother, when this consciousness襲ed my heart, it is best to go back to my hometown in one step, but can I quietly go back? I am not afraid of the neighbors' ridicule, but am I willing to step into this cage again and be a hooked fish? At this time, my thoughts, just like this tram, are bound by the rails and run back and forth, running, running, where will they end up?

Brother, what am I talking about?

(18) At the Restaurant

I jumped off the tram arbitrarily on the way, looking at the dim street lights in the center of the street,整理ing my steps, one lamp, two lamps, countless lamps, it is the lively center of Shanghai again.

"Wine", a gold-lettered black-bottomed city sign, rippled in the light and jumped into my eyes, and my disturbed nerves seemed to need its stimulation, "Go get drunk," I couldn't help but step into the restaurant. After occupying a table near the road and the waiter送ing the wine, I only took a small sip,擎ed the wine glass, and kept looking at the road in front, but what can I see? The lively urban area of Shanghai, at this time, is like a vast desert where no one has been seen for hundreds of miles to me. Can this fragile heart overcome such an environment? There is no beautiful smile of the sun here, but the same human beings, but the eyes of different people, those eyes are as terrible as the electric torches on cars. My future, "Can I bring a younger brother who has no experience and no productivity?" Mount Tai-like questions拥涌ed in my heart, going back to protect my younger brother, or bringing him to the desert to discover clear springs?

The neon lights were shining opposite, the cars were roaring in the center of the road, and the sound of mixed and happy leather shoes came from the stairs behind. I estimated that it was a group of students who were amazing at spending money. I don't know what movie they watched and散场ed from a sensual dance. After gorging themselves, they are preparing to spend the steps of the sleepless night. For a while, it seemed that the active air of youth was filling the small restaurant, and the romantic life of my school days restored in my memory, "There is always an opportunity for you young people!" Sister Hui's catchphrase powerfully束ed my scattered thoughts,忘形地擎ed the cup and drank the cold wine in one gulp.
